play true 是公司内部的文化和会一直坚持的精神，我们相信不管是生活，从事竞技体育还是创业都要堂堂正正地用心做。公司里没有等级，没有政治，每一份付出，努力和进步都会被尊重。

公司简介： 
通过体育竞技类游戏，体育资讯，赛事直播，球迷社区，体育数据收集，打造成移动互联网体育平台，从而丰富了关注和热爱体育人群的娱乐和社交互动的需求。我们要创造一个最新形式的体育竞猜方式，首先会做一款基于微信H5的NBA竞猜平台。团队成员有多年国内知名互联网公司的工作经验，我们的项目也拥有国内两家上市游戏公司back up。

What do we do?
At Daniel Wellington, unprecedented technical challenges are always coming down our way when our business keeps hitting new records. And that’s why we strive to solve business problems with innovative applications on scalable cloud infrastructure and leading-edge models. And we never bother stop improving our work and mindset as new tech stuff is developing around the globe every day. We run most of stuff on AWS Global/China while we’re also looking at Aliyun for better service availability in China region and play our magic with container (AWS ECS), serverless runtime(AWS Lambda) ,Redis, Varnish, Nginx, Apache, Databases (MySQL, Aurora, Postgre,NoSQL), Jira, and Jenkins.  
 
What you’ll be doing here  
We are looking for a DevOps Engineer with relevant experience who wants to join and automate our environments, further develop our delivery pipelines and build our monitoring. You will also be involved in on-call routine making sure that our official websites and other business systems are running properly to support the businesses. Part of the service involves writing your own tools and actions that run in our environments and it is therefore a requirement that you have documented experience of at least one, but preferably more, of the following languages: Go, Python, Ruby, JavaScript (node.js )
 
Who we hope you are
·Full working proficiency in Mandarin Chinese
·Proven English reading and writing skills
·Academic degree in computer science or related
·Experience of Managing Large Server Environments with a focus on Linux (Ubuntu)
·Experience of Web Servers (Apache, Nginx)
·Experience of Databases (MySQL, PostgreSQL)
·Experience of Cache and Reverse Proxys (Varnish, Memcached,Redis)
·Mastering of one or more programming languages and pursuit to automated process
·Problem-solver with proven record
·Able to do on-call if needed
 
What we would love to see from you
·Experience of AWS or Aliyun is strongly preferred
·Experience of the following AWS services (or equivalent cloud services) is strongly preferred: AWS ECS, AWS Lambda, AWS DynamoDB, API Gateway.
·Knowledge of JavaScript(Node.js)
·Knowledge of Go language
·Experience of Deployment(preferably continuous integration with Jenkins)
·Knowledge of SOA, Microservices, APIs.
·Thrive to learn new technology, take challenges and solve problems
 
What we offer at Daniel Wellington Business Technology
·   Competitive salary
·   A young, vibrant, international working environment
·   hands-on experience on leading-edge technology (Cisco Cloud networking, Aliyun, Amazon Web Services and etc).
·   Personalized training & career development based on your specialization and interest.
·   Full set of gadgets
·   Working at our newly renovated office with unbeatable ocean view
 
In this job you get to work in a fast-paced and rapid-growing environment where you need to be flexible day to day. You will spend your days with a highly skilled tech team who are all ambitious and who loves to do a great job. And have fun while doing so. We have a short decision-taking process so that we move forward fast as a company. We want you to come in, take ownership of your area of responsibility and support our fast-growing company reaching its new levels. If you’re the right person we will offer you a great role, in a fun company with great benefits. Join us in our exciting journey ahead.
 
If this sounds challenging and exciting do not hesitate to send your CV and personal letter.

微回收

靠谱：低承诺高兑现，先完成后优化，承诺做不到主动请吃鸡翅，或者选择被鄙视人品问题

微回收的闲置二手回收平台。闲置交易领域是有望诞生下一个数百亿美金市值公司的领域，目前腾讯阿里均在布局，具有极高的市场空间和进入门槛。在与腾讯合作后，转转将成为腾讯社区内默认的闲置交易工具。

-计算机及相关专业本科以上学历
-3年以上前端开发经验，负责过复杂应用的前端设计和开发

4111314 20k-40k
基于 KVM 提供的虚拟化管理平台，是 SmartX 提供的核心产品之一。它提供强大且易用的虚拟机管理功能，并支持虚拟机高可用，定时快照保护，异地容灾备份等高级功能。除此之外，SmartX 的虚拟化管理平台还可以对非 KVM 平台的虚拟机或容器进行统一管理和调度。
作为虚拟化管理平台方向的工程师，你将接触最先进的虚拟化技术，完善和优化复杂的虚拟机管理系统，资源调度系统和高可用系统。你编写的软件将帮助客户实现高效，敏捷的 IT 基础设施。通过技术的手段，提高世界企业IT能力，让IT更简单！
Responsibilities：
- 设计、开发基于 KVM，VMware，Xenserver，Docker 等虚拟化技术的统一管理平台；
- 设计、开发大规模集群的异步任务调度中心，提供高并发且稳定的调度功能；
- 设计、开发基于 KVM 虚拟机高可用（HA）功能，保证用户业务的连续性；
- 设计并实现健壮，清晰的 RESTful API；
- 撰写细致的设计文档，并对其他同事的代码进行审查；
- 与测试、产品、售前和售后部门密切配合，不断提升产品质量和竞争力。
Minimum Qualifications：
- 热爱编程，具有以下任一种语言的扎实的编程经验：Python、Golang、Java；
- 具有 web 后台开发经验；
- 具有基于以下至少一种软件开发的经验，包括 MySQL、MongoDB、Redis、Cassandra、ElasticSearch、Zookeeper 等；
- 熟悉 Linux 环境编程，理解 I/O 模型、事件模型、协程、线程池等基本概念，具有异步网络编程经验；
- 具有独立完成复杂功能的经历，能够完成完备的设计文档，清晰的接口定义，能够有效的进行任务拆分；
- 代码风格干净简洁，具有极高的软件质量标准。
Preferred Qualifications：
- 有大规模集群系统的开发经验，对软件高可用，高并发有深刻的理解；
- 有基于 KVM，Qemu，Libvirt 等项目开发的经验；
- 有 Openstack 的开发经验。
我们提供：
- 标配的五险一金和极具竞争力的薪水，持续的期权机制；
- 各种水果零食、咖啡牛奶无限量免费供应，任君挑选；
- 每年十二天带薪年假，旅游工作两不误；
- 补充医疗保险，为你健康保驾护航；
- 弹性工作时间，为结果负责；
- 年度旅游&定期团建活动。
